 - [https://phys.org/news/2024-04-genetic-underpinnings-environmental-stress.html](https://phys.org/news/2024-04-genetic-underpinnings-environmental-stress.html)
 - RSS feed: 
 - date published: 2024-04-11T20:01:13.642553+00:00

Plants can be temperamental. Even weeds along the side of highways or pushing their way up in the cracks of concrete sidewalks can get stressed out by dehydration, cold, excess salt and more.
